Version 2.0		 Version 2.0 Module 4: External Agency Reporting 21-Nov-08 0               v1.5.1 Mayo has run into an issue where they have an AdEERS report they are re-entering into caAERS and the Prior Therapy is a Chemotherapy which requires (in caAERS) to have an Agent. The problem is they don't have an agent but they were able to submit to AdEERS successfully. Jennifer has confirmed that via the AdEERS UI Agent is not required. ---------------------update------------------------------------
After debugging with sameer, The following scenario seems reproducible
1>Create an observed AE and manually add it to 10 day CTEP report and submit it
2> Come back to CAE>>Adverse events flow [The R icon will show for the submitted AE]
3> Add a new observed AE with low grade [no rules are fired]
4> IN review and report page add this AE into the amend submitted 10 report
5> After reaching the reporter tab in the expedited AE flow, do not continue
6> Click on Enter AEs tab and go to CAE>>Adverse events flow and do not change the data.
7> The R icon is shown beside the new observed AE which has not yes been submitted
8> WHen user clicks continue, the pop up for amend report is shown although user has not changed any detials in the the CAE>>Adverse Events tab.
9> This pop up should not be shown
